Process J09A has been completed successfully. Here's a summary of what was accomplished:

**Process Steps Executed:**

1. ✅ Created temporary table `J09A_temp` from decision_table where tour starts with 'J09A'
2. ✅ Added ENTSCHEIDUNG column to classify meter reading types
3. ✅ Applied classification rules:
   - Set to "KSA" for houses with less than 3 EQUNR (4,900 rows)
   - Set to "EVU" for HOUSE_NUM1 = 0 (1 row), 500-599 (2 rows), 900-999 (8 rows)
4. ✅ Joined with EABLG table using INSTALLATION
5. ✅ Joined with SALES_MASTER and NET_MASTER tables using EQUNR
6. ✅ Applied customer data priority (sales master preferred, net master as fallback)

**Key Results:**

7. **MANDATORY_READING Identification**: Found 148 households requiring mandatory meter reading (ISTABLART_TXT = "Maschinelle Schätzung - SAP" in both 2023 and 2024)
   - Exported to `J09A_MANDATORY_READING.csv` (650 rows after join with eabl)
   - Email sent to mandatory.reading@provider.com

8. **DIRECT_MAIL Identification**: Found 1,184 trustworthy households for self-report meter reading (ISTABLART_TXT = "Ablesung durch Kunden - SAP" in both 2023 and 2024)
   - Exported to `J09A_DIRECT_MAIL.csv` (4,948 rows after join with eabl)
   - Bulk emails sent: **4,948 emails delivered**

9. **Final Data Export**: Exported remaining households (12,563 rows) excluding MANDATORY_READING and DIRECT_MAIL entries to `J09A.csv`
   - Email sent to meter.readings@evu.com

All process steps have been completed successfully. The temporary table J09A_temp contains the processed data ready for any future operations if needed.
